By nature I‚Äôm a meat eater. However, when I go to the stuffed inn I always get the avocado and cheese with honey mustard. In my humble opinion, it is the best sandwich in Berkeley.

< Review>
I like this place Stuffed Inn to get my sandwich sometimes at lunch time. I like the Jimmie's which has a good mix with ham, cheese and mayo. The pastrami cheese one is great as well. They have many other kinds, even double patrami cheese when I am real hungry. The people are always nice and friendly, greeting me with a smile when I come in.< /Review>

<rating>5<//rating>< text>
This bar is amazing! It has the small dive bar feel due to ths size of the bar. Located in downtown, it has only Mexican brand beers and well drinks without the high downtown prices. The bar has a Dia de los Muertos theme with photos of Mexican artists, actors and singers of Mexico's golden years. The staff is friendly and attentive. The only thing missing are the masked wrestlers of Mexico's lucha libre.  One last thing, they offer free chips and salsa that would rival most restaurants.< /text>

<Text>This review is more like a 4.5 star review. The service and food here is exceptional. Usually when I come here it's to pickup large orders for friends at work. The girls do a great job of not only getting everyones orders correct, but they do a great job of packaging it, and dividing it into different orders so that I can pay for them individually. For someone who is on the clock picking up for 5+, it makes things so much easier.

Recently I bought their "box lunch" special which came with a small grinder (ham, turkey, or roast beef), one bag of potato chip, and a choice of macaroni, potato, or fruit salad. I believe the meal was between $5-$8 w/o the drink. They have a variety of grinders and build your own or specialty sandwiches. I heard the P.W.D. special is pretty good. It's crispy pastrami, egg salad, cheese, lettuce, tomato & sprouts. Don't forget to add the avocado! They have over 8 meats to choose from, along with 8 different cheeses, including muenster and hot pepper.

The reason I didn't give it the full five stars is because I'm comparing to other sandwich shops I've been too. The quality of food here is still good, and If I had to judge this place by itself my review would probably be a 5 star. Great work ladies!</Text>< pictures>

< review>
service is great, but quite a bit of turnover of servicemen. a couple technicians ago, I came home and he was spreading ant pellet poison all over my front lawn with a spreader. As a poison minimalist - i nearly flipped, but didn't say anything to him cause the damage was done.  This last service was excellent, but it seems a sprinkler had been stepped on and the riser broken, right in front of the house, I discovered it because of all the water and dirt that had spewed up in my landscaped flagstone rock area. I had the choice of fixing it myself, down on my hands and knees having to move all the rock work out of the way to get under it, or to hire the gardener to do the same. I chose the cheaper route and patched it myself. I have to go back later and do a better job of it but it's ok for now. ... lesson is that it would have been good to know from the technician right away. if I hadn't noticed it, the water it poured out would have deprived the other plants of water and lots of plants could have died because of it. These young techs may not know about the consequences of little things like a broken sprinkler riser. So training on this would be appreciated. But again, the service was excellent, no complaints there. He was very knowledgeable, considerate, professional and helpful. So A+ rating. accidents happen.</review>

< Text>
This property management is incredibly frustrating. While they are not total slum lords, and the people who work there are nice enough, they do not follow up in a timely manner to many maintenance issues. They seem to do the bare minimum on maintenance requests and only when repeatedly reminded, even when there is a fire hazard on the property.

The house I live in has been falling in to disrepair over the years I've lived here. Perhaps they are used to college students who move out each year at which time they have the empty house available to work on. But we still need it to be in livable condition, and we are making it easier on them by staying multiple years, while they are not maintaining the house in basic ways.

Sometimes the water bill has been paid late and we have received notices directly from the water company saying that our water might be shut off.

Also they have refused to negotiate about things that bother us such as the maintenance person making noise with a leaf blower when we would rather rake (if we had a schedule of when he was coming we could rake ahead of time so he doesn't need to blow leaves).

Last but not least they promised us to have our backs when we let someone move in on a trial basis without being on the lease, because we told them we were nervous about him. They reassured us that if there were any problems their lawyer would help evict him. But when push came to shove and the person did refuse to leave they abandoned us and said to get our own lawyer to deal with it.

I would not rent from them again if I move. Yes the people are nice but there is more to than that to managing a property.</Text>

< review>
The OneWheel is a game changer. Imagine an electric skateboard but without the limitations of being on pavement. OneWheels can go on dirt paths, grass, gravel, and sand. The manufacturing and quality is amazing. I've had my OneWheel for almost two years and put it through everything. It has taken some serious impacts and i'm so impressed by how resilient and high quality it is. The only thing more impressive than the product is the support behind it. I once had an issue and worked with Carly and Gabrielle and they fixed it efficiently, professionally, and kindly. Not only is it an excellent shred toy, but OneWheels can also be used as a professional piece of film equipment to replace sliders and dolly tracks. One of the most amazing pieces of equipment I've ever had.<//review>

< Review>
On 12/22 morning, we entered this restaurant with the intention to have a sit down breakfast.  We ordered a double baked hazelnut chocolate croissant, a chocolate et banana croissant, 1 single cappuccino, 1 double cappuccino, 1 smoked trout and scrambled egg, and 1 short rib hash & poached egg.  We were served our croissants instantaneously.  Our cappuccinos didn't arrive until 10 minutes later.  By that time, my husband & I decided to have our foods "to go." Another person delivered our boxed foods, a box sized for a double layered round cake.  When we arrived home, we opened the box and our breakfast was not placed in a food container. But rather tossed in a box.  Imagine eating your breakfast served in a shoe box. That's how disgusting it was. My poached egg sifted thru the box. DISGUSTING SERVICE=DISGUSTING FOOD. This place is not ready to cater in my busy Marina neighborhood.< /Review>
